namespace = colonize_it_create

country_event = {
	id = colonize_it_create.0
	title = colonize_it_create.0.t
	desc = colonize_it_create.0.d
	picture = DEBATE_REPUBLICAN_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "miss_click"
	}
}
country_event = { #インドネシア1
	id = colonize_it_create.1
	title = trade_company
	desc = indonesia
	picture = none
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = Z01
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.2
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_indonesia_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = Z01
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = Z01
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = Z01
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		Z01 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_indonesia
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #北海1
	id = colonize_it_create.26
	title = trade_company
	desc = north_sea
	picture = none
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = Z31
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.27
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_north_sea_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = Z31
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = Z31
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = Z31
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		Z31 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_north_sea
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

	after = {
		Z43 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_bordeaux
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				exists = Z56
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.52
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_valencia_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = Z56
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = Z56
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = Z56
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		Z56 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_valencia
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_genua
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

				id = colonize_it_create.65
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_genua_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = Z69
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = Z69
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = Z69
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {

				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government

country_event = { #バルト4
	id = colonize_it_create.89
	title = baltic_sea
	desc = trade_company
	picture = none
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = Z94
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.90
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_baltic_sea_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = Z94
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = Z94
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = Z94
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		Z94 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_baltic_sea
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = X20
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.115
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_kiev_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = X20
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = X20
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = X20
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		X20 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_kiev
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_kazan
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}

				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = X45
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = X45
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = X45
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		X45 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_constantinople
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

	title = basra
	desc = trade_company

	hidden = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = X58
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.153
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_basra_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = X58
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = X58
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = X58
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		X58 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_basra

				}
				release = X83

country_event = { #タンザニア2
	id = colonize_it_create.202
	title = great_lakes
	desc = trade_company
	picture = none
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = Y09
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.203
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_great_lakes_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = Y09
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = Y09
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = Y09
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		Y09 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_great_lakes
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

	id = colonize_it_create.227
	title = west_india
	desc = trade_company
	picture = none
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = Y34
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.228
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_west_india_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = Y34
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = Y34
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = Y34
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		Y34 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_west_india
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_deccan
		}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = Y59
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.253
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_samarkand_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = Y59
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = Y59
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = Y59
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		Y59 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_samarkand
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_yumen
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}

					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = Y84
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = Y84
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {

				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}

			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_south_china
		}

	id = colonize_it_create.290
	title = south_china
	desc = trade_company
	picture = none
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = Y97
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.0
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_south_china_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = Y97
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = Y97
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = Y97
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		Y97 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim

country_event = { #ニジェール5
	id = colonize_it_create.315
	title = katsina
	desc = trade_company
	picture = none
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = W23
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.0
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_katsina_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = W23
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = W23
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = W23
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		W23 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_katsina
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.0
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_eastern_america_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = W83
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = W83
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = W83
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		W83 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_eastern_america
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}

			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_colombia
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #コロンビア3
	id = colonize_it_create.353
	title = colombia
	desc = colonial
	picture = none
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = W96
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.354
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_colombia_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = W96
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = W96
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = W96
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		W96 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_trade_company_region
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_tag_colombia

	id = colonize_it_create.378
	title = korea
	desc = region
	picture = none
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = T08
			}
			country_event = {
				id = colonize_it_create.379
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = colonize_it_korea_colony
			event_target:colonize_it_target = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
					}
					remove_core = event_target:colonize_it_target
					add_core = T08
					clr_province_flag = colonize_it_mark
				}
				release = T08
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = T08
			}
			clear_global_event_target = colonize_it_target
		}
	}
	option = {}
	after = {
		T08 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = colonize_it_expansion }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = colonize_it_expansion
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = colonize_it_target
			change_government = republic
			add_government_reform = colonial_government
			add_manpower = 25
			add_treasury = 250
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
				}
				clr_country_flag = colonize_it_regulation_claim
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = colonize_it_religion.2
		}
	}
}
